deprecate_posargs(deprecation_warning, remappable_names, /):\n101:     \"\"\"\n102:     Function/method decorator to deprecate some or all positional arguments.\n103: \n104:     The decorated function RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS: Maximum number of requests per window (default: 100)\n    - RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW: Time window in seconds (default: 3600)\n\n    Uses Django's cache framework to track request counts per IP address.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, get_response):\n        super().__init__(get_response)\n        self.rate_limit_requests = getattr(\n            settings, \"RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS\", 100\n        )\n        self.rate_limit_window = getattr(\n            settings, \"RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW\", 3600\n        )\n\n    def process_request(self, request):\n        \"\"\"\n        Check if the client IP has exceeded the rate limit.\n\n        Returns HttpResponseTooManyRequests (429) if limit exceeded,\n        otherwise returns None to continue request processing.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Get client IP from request\n        client_ip = request.META.get(\"REMOTE_ADDR\", \"unknown\")\n\n        # Create a unique cache key for this IP\n        cache_key = f\"rate_limit:{client_ip}\"\n\n        # Get current request count from cache\n        request_count = cache.get(cache_key, 0)\n\n        # Check if limit has been exceeded\n        if request_count >= self.rate_limit_requests:\n            return HttpResponseTooManyRequests()\n\n        # Increment the request count\n        cache.set(\n            cache_key,\n            request_count + 1,\n            self.rate_limit_window\n        )\n\n        # Continue with normal request processing\n        return None\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":6,"cache_creation_input_tokens":602,"cache_read_input_tokens":76232,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":602},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"6bf971dc-b847-44cb-84ab-f9354e6d3be0","uuid":"b6f605ba-b06b-40da-b83d-ff2117a0962e"}

Next request should return 429\n        request = self.factory.get(\"/\")\n        request.META[\"REMOTE_ADDR\"] = \"10.0.0.1\"\n        response = middleware.process_request(request)\n\n        self.assertIsInstance(response, HttpResponseTooManyRequests)\n        self.assertEqual(response.status_code, 429)\n\n    @override_settings(RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS=3, RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW=3600)\n    def test_missing_remote_addr(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that missing REMOTE_ADDR is handled gracefully.\"\"\"\n        middleware = RateLimitMiddleware(get_response)\n\n        # Make more requests without REMOTE_ADDR\n        for i in range(2):\n            request = self.factory.get(\"/\")\n            response = middleware.process_request(request)\n            self.assertIsNone(response)\n\n        # (This check may be somewhat expensive,\n53:             # so we only do it if we already know we're sending a redirect,\n54:             # or in process_response if we get a 404.)\n55:             if self.should_redirect_with_slash(request):\n56:                 path = self.get_full_path_with_slash(request)\n57:             else:\n58:                 path = request.get_full_path()\n59: \n60:             return self.response_redirect_class(f\"{request.scheme}://www.{host}{path}\")\n61: \n62:     def should_redirect_with_slash(self, request):\n63:         \"\"\"\n64:         Return True if settings.APPEND_SLASH is True and appending a slash to\n65:         the request path turns an invalid path into a valid one.\n66:         \"\"\"\n67:         if settings.APPEND_SLASH and not request.path_info.endswith(\"/\"):\n68:             urlconf = getattr(request, \"urlconf\", None)\n69:             if not is_valid_path(request.path_info, urlconf):\n70:                 match = is_valid_path(\"%s/\" % request.path_info, urlconf)\n71:                 if match:\n72:                     view = match.func\n73:                     return getattr(view, \"should_append_slash\", True)\n74:         return False\n75: \n76:     def get_full_path_with_slash(self, request):\n77:         \"\"\"\n78:         Return the full path of the request with a trailing slash appended.\n79: \n80:         Raise a RuntimeError if settings.DEBUG is True and request.method is\n81: ","url":"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/sg-evals/django--674eda1c@674eda1c03a3187905f48afee0f15226aa62fdf3/-/blob/django/middleware/common.py%3FL1-80"}}}
